msg:It's quite comfortable overall. The service staff in the housekeeping depar**ent and the front desk lady are very nice. The facilities in the room are more user-friendly and suitable for staying with the elderly and children.
To be honest, I personally don't recommend eating breakfast in the hotel here. It ends at 7 to 9 o'clock. In fact, Wuhan is famous for its early breakfast culture. You can get up and go out to find a breakfast shop to eat. The business reception here may be done earlier, which is not suitable for people who go out to play... Hahaha, who wants to get up early on vacation?

For friends who come here to travel, if you want to leave from the hotel, it is recommended that you call a taxi about 15 minutes in advance (there will be traffic jams half an hour before dinner time).
Finally, it is recommended to strengthen the cleaning and deodorization of the room.
